    "## 支架安装没有水平，矫正平台和地面夹角，沿z轴对xy平面进行旋转\n",
    "### \\$x'=x\\cdot\\cos{\\theta} + y \\cdot \\sin{\\theta}$\n",
    "\n",
    "### \\$y'=y\\cdot\\cos{\\theta} - x \\cdot \\sin{\\theta}$"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 4,
   "id": "ba3d8059-88cf-4914-93f1-f80305b571ac",
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "theta = -1.4\n",
    "pi=3.1415926535898\n",
    "x = d100[:,1]*np.cos(theta/180*pi) + d100[:,2]*np.sin(theta/180*pi)\n",
    "y = d100[:,2]*np.cos(theta/180*pi) - d100[:,1]*np.sin(theta/180*pi)\n",
    "z = d100[:,3]"
   ]
